BEGIN=============================================================================================
LogMessageType:SqlError
DateTime:2020-08-26 08:03:55.874
UseService:True
ConnectionName:
NetCode:NETOFFICE
ExecuteType:Text
TakeTime:Milliseconds:4.0002
Sql:SELECT TOP 200 Bas_MO.MOId,
			   Bas_MO.MOCode,
			   Bas_Item.ItemCode,
			   Bas_Item.ItemName+'/'+Bas_Item.ItemDesc as 'ItemName',
			   Bas_Order.OrderCode,
			   Bas_Customer.CustomerCode
FROM Bas_MO WITH(NOLOCK) 
LEFT JOIN dbo.Bas_Item  WITH(NOLOCK) ON dbo.Bas_Item.ItemId = dbo.Bas_MO.ItemId
LEFT JOIN dbo.Bas_OrderDetail  WITH(NOLOCK) ON dbo.Bas_OrderDetail.OrderDetailId = dbo.Bas_MO.OrderDetailId
LEFT JOIN dbo.Bas_Order  WITH(NOLOCK) ON dbo.Bas_Order.OrderId = dbo.Bas_OrderDetail.OrderId
LEFT JOIN dbo.Bas_Customer  WITH(NOLOCK) ON dbo.Bas_Customer.CustomerId = dbo.Bas_MO.CustomerId
WHERE Bas_MO.MOId=ISNULL(@Id,Bas_MO.MOId)
AND Bas_MO.MOCode LIKE '%'+ISNULL(@MOCode,Bas_MO.MOCode)+'%'
AND (@ItemId IS NULL OR Bas_MO.ItemId=@ItemId)
AND (ISNULL(@OrderCode,'')='' OR (ISNULL(@OrderCode,'')!='' AND Bas_Order.OrderCode LIKE '%'+ISNULL(@OrderCode,Bas_Order.OrderCode)+'%'))
AND (@CustomerId IS NULL OR Bas_MO.CustomerId=@CustomerId)
ORDER BY Bas_MO.MOCode
Params:
@Id=DBNull
@MOCode=
@ItemId=null
@CustomerId=null
@OrderCode=null
END===============================================================================================

Sql:SELECT TOP 200 Bas_MO.MOId,
			   Bas_MO.MOCode,
			   Bas_Item.ItemCode,
			   Bas_Item.ItemName+'/'+Bas_Item.ItemDesc as 'ItemName',
			   Bas_Order.OrderCode,
			   Bas_Customer.CustomerCode
FROM Bas_MO WITH(NOLOCK) 
LEFT JOIN dbo.Bas_Item  WITH(NOLOCK) ON dbo.Bas_Item.ItemId = dbo.Bas_MO.ItemId
LEFT JOIN dbo.Bas_OrderDetail  WITH(NOLOCK) ON dbo.Bas_OrderDetail.OrderDetailId = dbo.Bas_MO.OrderDetailId
LEFT JOIN dbo.Bas_Order  WITH(NOLOCK) ON dbo.Bas_Order.OrderId = dbo.Bas_OrderDetail.OrderId
LEFT JOIN dbo.Bas_Customer  WITH(NOLOCK) ON dbo.Bas_Customer.CustomerId = dbo.Bas_MO.CustomerId
WHERE Bas_MO.MOId=ISNULL(@Id,Bas_MO.MOId)
AND Bas_MO.MOCode LIKE '%'+ISNULL(@MOCode,Bas_MO.MOCode)+'%'
AND (@ItemId IS NULL OR Bas_MO.ItemId=@ItemId)
AND (ISNULL(@OrderCode,'')='' OR (ISNULL(@OrderCode,'')!='' AND Bas_Order.OrderCode LIKE '%'+ISNULL(@OrderCode,Bas_Order.OrderCode)+'%'))
AND (@CustomerId IS NULL OR Bas_MO.CustomerId=@CustomerId)
ORDER BY Bas_MO.MOCode

			   Bas_MO.DeviceType,
			   Bas_MO.IsCanVirtualInput,
			   Bas_MO.SideAFeedingStationTableId,
			   Bas_MO.SideBFeedingStationTableId,
			   Bas_MO.RowVersion,
			   Bas_MO.NetWeight,
			   Bas_MO.GrossWeight
FROM Bas_MO WITH(NOLOCK) 
LEFT JOIN dbo.Bas_Item  WITH(NOLOCK) ON dbo.Bas_Item.ItemId = dbo.Bas_MO.ItemId
LEFT JOIN dbo.Bas_OrderDetail  WITH(NOLOCK) ON dbo.Bas_OrderDetail.OrderDetailId = dbo.Bas_MO.OrderDetailId
LEFT JOIN dbo.Bas_Order  WITH(NOLOCK) ON dbo.Bas_Order.OrderId = dbo.Bas_OrderDetail.OrderId
WHERE Bas_MO.MOId=ISNULL(@Id,Bas_MO.MOId)
AND Bas_MO.MOCode=ISNULL(@Text,Bas_MO.MOCode)
Params:

@CpuID=BFEBFBFF000306C3

@Id=190
@Text=DBNull
@ParentId=DBNull
@Return_Message=DBNull
@ReturnValue=DBNull
END===============================================================================================
